Programmatic Brand

 

The Wall Street Journal looks at the auction for Forbes Media, which is hoping that its positioning as a digital media brand pays off. The WSJ's William Launder writes, "The path to success for digital media companies, even ones untethered to a legacy magazine, is far from certain, digital media executives and analysts say. The rise of so-called programmatic ad buying, which allows ad buyers to purchase digital inventory using exchange-like technology, has undercut the profitability of traditional banner display ads." Read it (subscription) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd0EtdP9av41wLLCSZKEqWDcgjoSVWssrPFDL0FChDGV5DMi_xVBcUgXIx_DuD6LPHk_0w_MfJ8BIQ6i9YDhK02jq8ZfDkgdCkHtea4f3c5Dhna3ECIghfUujIOtlin0M8Osi7mqzVqXo_164-tqWhLarh-0IqOcNtaLsa9Q0UPvC7rQgtNR93Ipk61aaHAmsmQ=> .

 

Real-Time Funds

 

A new SEC filing <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd1-mApqYT4Zyl8kT1QUPeL1UGmbnF3FkZFjSktNpe40ke0c0X-cWXW9cby0QsmqXyXqhYRtsgPkk5hdz61nx2mkpFbZdMShmLIAOFz77Wklbk5GcDKYF8QBYfHX1Waa8xMCnmYNpm4VFbbRim0Gd_e1KSFTBZfrfuRwTMutztmiV6Z7C_vo6aPlqrZ7bgxoe4x32Uc75JlicJ1E6yzm9pGZ>  records a $5 million investment in real-time analytics firm MetaMarkets. CEO Michael Driscoll tells VentureBeat about the new funds, "It was a relatively small amount, but enough to help us continue to focus on accelerating our business without making the time commitment required by raising a new round of funding." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd2_iRu8OpzyV-MnFLp9iQBMyeHB9eeJlBC9cAwBZnx7N5as3NztdcYc1a4s97nouGK8XjyiuByNpzW0E9wahSvOuHM7Bp6DOdzLobeCw5EdleoEZ8uGBzpHjq96JgEJaok1eaxeY_aAB4D-o0N2vA-iLArVECBDrzuKCWWecHWrHYwnIxTNOQ4xxEc_APK0rTuqSisPTMpWnQ==> .

 

News Buy

 

News Corp. has acquired social news site Storyful for $25 million, according to a press release. "Storyful has become the village square for valuable video, using journalistic sensibility, integrity and creativity to find, authenticate and commercialize user-generated content," said Robert Thomson, chief executive of News Corp. "Through this acquisition, we can extend the village square across borders, languages and platforms." Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd19uRdbxRdi1ks-w25QypbVVYU_r_MVku_Xj15GjoJKEOD8OroxHw510bKlwt-lUojyKzWcR96oZgVRbsy6sjJrkxz54Ls6euy-JYU9v4edfvMyaA1RK_dpoR3iNUlBQj9TcJ4LhjZyqrvKdOmNkNaxdbzXqEEcz81T_oCh7gQNkmmowzB1ko9Pgk73LGLNMyY=> .

 

Twitter's Mobile Lifeline

 

Mobile ad startup MoPub offers Twitter a safety net if the newly public company doesn't quite hit its expected stride, reports AllThingsD's Peter Kafka. Although MoPub's recent launch of native ad units available to advertisers in its marketplace does not yet incorporate Twitter data, it's possible to see how Twitter is extending its position to develop a true mobile ad network. And MoPub has been more than doubling its revenue over the last few quarters from a year prior. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd2aRQtLFvp0UuVoqPPQr8Izcq69w0CqTYKtUDrQgQhqHfABUmWjDbD7dtgWVtzobqmQzFFl-bABrl2TtrCAfPDyrfAceQ6qwv5mdUIXM72isf5iwT4I_bZZ8ye5XuF9gcsed8r_lHKnjZxdpzrb4fV72NV7ZTkHtChiWy--pe-dujGvP99VHG8KaT-1vSMCwokvurESuKavaJmwunNTQeiH> .

 

Social Media In China

 

Social media companies from the United States have a hard time breaking into the Chinese market, but Ad Age predicts the possibility of LinkedIn doing well. "People on LinkedIn talk about their professional life, their work, news about their industries, it's not that sensitive," said Xiaofeng Wang, a Forrester Research analyst who thinks LinkedIn has potential in China. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd2Rf8fSLnLwubDdKnyX2C6HWzmiNxJ9T9tUmBgmj86sLjc2SZoQ0W2apTOr8T_NqVtBRGeYvTRhh5nnOnzQ-0DjqB5M0Je9qnu_jNhSZjyXULRlEPzByLk_3newGYEA1wlnSfwgFKnsi4oToYpGKSl_yPqHxv9JweIhlRT26zJMMFFt5qu7kBxwf-vQw7B-Ohs=> .

The New Toy Store

 

Toys R Us is trying to make mobile shopping easier by adding a voice-recognition and product-recommendation option to its app, Mobile Commerce Daily is reporting. Shoppers will be able to tell the app certain information about the child they are shopping for and the app will recommend a product. "At Zoove, we see consumer engagement rates skyrocket when there is a voice on the other end - even if it is automated technology - it offers a form of personalization and human connection that SMS messaging and email cannot provide," said Ashley Eckel, head of marketing at Zoove. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd14pbXZdTWhkYcI45zAJivAveLKFilVFj3Dgzj1hKDFUGGY4hY5Wsp5qxWDS6w3iXDARoF0hhJ_Q60f27NdjpsreRo6UURJ6nAM-sKC5qjPynz-vTh97BZa6dNM0LvevX_-5aVTMDe5QXHkR3zopYf5SOGY5qiL65JDt0kBjy_DpuTMmk9eHVGKwfaOe-DEbryMXUvdLoVeGudanO0TQpbE85GIs7y45S9uQgqUXEylgHd_sglB6wvv> .

 

WPP On A Spree

 

Holding company WPP PLC has been on a massive holiday buying spree. On Friday, the company announced <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd1TTtIkZq1sr_JxCECuBMLXh8dp_mMwAFKh-oCEI7WStAtQvJ797gpEwpA_6Z3zWgWahN5XB5V1xq3x8AS9vdAkXZtp63MCRgCyq1tQFTwoghzMTnIFeDtLSulo8jdxfDWCS25D-wC0WP4EjrlHe5JhVvF1p4bHP9nQQHAsFHcSfWCcDpizUBBCqywmKaVD3igJOJIT9zuA2Oba0uj0E7Xair3bk43MIK91HWG8LuCsHyduAEHxLUtO>  its intent to buy Philippines-based media agency MASSCOM. This follows Thursday's announcement that WPP's media management unit GroupM had agreed to a majority stake <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd3VmWucolWe5hb_w7KrM3O5oYs40LeqU7NInXMYJjG_UNPt0Xln5KTDwzNMYfBjpeN-Xpag5yb5N4cS3X3DIoyJYfzYo2VVyeQ6p26QsFf_dflX_KhVBBGQrQBs0E4-WWOqq3YFDyxYOAplKd2v9fFs97yTpNjcq56os_2SIHkz2JXJ2rRwKRK8orlRAfuSshq2GH5eUTc40bscxRvFboEia_7Phhwo-jEl9L6QwbFc1bJEonM3BZGx>  in ClickMedia. And on Wednesday, its subsidiary Grey acquired a majority stake <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd1rswlDi9MrAB4m6uH--md2aAr6p2Q5YI0jg1qr5rU9s2uO0H5MvHMqOvRaRLTXDzKlnjV6J0sUW3kPR5kcP9tJlDVmbMgCa698o2q7kiGfGkjNphyTQagljtW1PknMQnTnMKIW9kC3b3mUNL257thEs7IWzWohV2BOBTw89BYDBixa-V8O60gDcse-SqmJ-M1lOZKcqLDKe-8AN5f5mE-6g3wbVc_OgnjFqbFhTTaKx9MxyNDUa17mV8xeHEv2FP4lxUNDIQtj-w==>  in the rural marketing company RC&M. On that same day, its brand, media and communications research subsidiary Millward Brown acquired <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd2UsBjHYHJQyr0dQXgv6pucmbIoz7EFSTL1djOtTidmzknati1BXJq6BdiTUnwltWn0U62M2yUGvo2oo49jCc39PZoN-6gmGbGWBfRYhm8G2vhqNvV7KAjaJbTmaARgNq8Vft6BICEd6rRaSn1kBdkYgpeHI36UMbEVCO487FqyZcbXaMVPDggozbmUmCfhL5kpHWT-XurugO0R_J3lpJRyjRntSjZOg-t0Yt77oAB15QEGOXjyIEd8v0HnaRPbZoYKdhw6ZToNxKrbglSrktrs>  a majority stake in Russia-based research shop ARMI-Marketing. On Tuesday, WPP purchased a 30% <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd3WkkEHjBh8828CiKpAelXb128P2BXXYyUUsfFTI02Lq1xRft4FweJnOSyQ7wz858NWBWyVqtfPXiSU9OLZLdFng-9b25mKhJdtvwLorigDCjv9JikVOrhrztD29W-4NoE2orNhI0pIsXRQYVOxN42V-BWRAKLll4jCbnZJMBbyt2QsgC8ihL65bH50CasUkMDJjVdBsTK54jD8tBtN9cC_sKv0AEsKloXiCvdQRI50YA==>  stake in research consultancy Richard Attias & Associates. And on Monday, WPP's data investment management business Kantar agreed to acquire <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0015q9PhxScNd1RhYMGRKs8fmN9bUd3S1DTTQAUFD1-nLRza70fKDDfMdPSI6DUxBrsF35j5OxEMdIlrQI8scypt0Hb82cdPmH5BhTRITrFfZ5Xn0dr5HSKV5regOP4wnnEFUAST8Bx3GZn8qXCbCfkMaDRDwe07fCnKelNE0i2RuZ35WKt4b6RNpHIjJlaQi22VJCNtDmIe8Glr0apzcZUH8H16KuUYXYbcED0_zUCoGY=>  Singaporean media monitoring and analytics service Fisheye.

Now With More Engagement

 

Google has expanded the capabilities of its Engagement Ads <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001GseQtw40XEIRWzt-9WcTprPjWLV2oUl1pJe96I99SX6RQuEo7amdPccfH94SnJNtZTKY3MEFDcogp6Hyk9S_TA-aa7v4gwb-Qr1xlMYmQcd-j7kc6iAaT2vRIrG8mGT_tAoXVj-vM556V9m5UP116bU3khZB6AkoMj2ayzm7oFM=> , which run on the Google Display Network, are offered on a CPE (cost per engagement) basis and are more interactive than static banner ads. Engagement Ads now run across mobile devices and have a "shoppable" format, meaning users can purchase items directly within the ad itself. Just in time for that last-minute holiday buying binge. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001GseQtw40XELXLGU2XpyB-4J4Hpidj8w9cDL_k0Etcz6N0hq5eIPsr-h_o0iUn-e8oyK_soYKrPoI5aL5oCm8wZXT3msd7uuYGknYlcbsG27v4P8ZW6NR3Va5s-OZs0hkl97O_ivHWLtFSCG6Pd1LLY-ynY2K1-CgT7TECLnl8fQy9mvvNyApT8lF-UGgeSv_>  on Google's blog.

 

Native Advertising In The NYT

 

Amid controversy around The New York Times' January rollout of a digital native-advertising product, publisher Arthur Sulzberger Jr. emphasized in a letter to newspaper employees that there would be "strict separation between the newsroom and the job of creating content for the new native ads.'' In other words, he plans to slap on all sorts of labels and visual cues to differentiate paid content from editorial. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001GseQtw40XEJZQwaxw-LRIj969HrxqQ1uZC_RszN7fxvdF-vu71diXkoSeMU6uRy15-ldekNj6BHn9Z8CH_EtLQCfRQE2h-EqhVsxGzKv_P-ky8eiPKpYcPBwMtpQyswQPJpC74ofqOGHNcSo3_jzYokva_pws21rVfOvqPSlVe7hJzXrhfLj6p79XxeLFlwMKLx8sMBFM2YU2YWoWigGbbTGyUm-qP7Ox9c-DIloZzd6bvMUC13lTpKUo4Dg4TL-> .

 

Innovation Pays Off

 

Foursquare has introduced multiple monetization options this year and it has "paid" off, as the company just raised $35 million in a Series D round, according to AllThingsD. "I think we are really delivering on the promises we made with the recommendations service and we had a better case when after we were able to get it out there for everyone to see," said COO Evan Cohen. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001GseQtw40XEL1bjH_LonlNnAU5bHFcj1V8bfJyTM6OmDBP2lgF_4CbA2h2beOO7U_t-JJidlxcmTa6Sc9Ohoh56D07LQK2WKkYoQrgb75VA5VWhpP-rPr8M2MpIZ6X4fJxnbGaOnW3ALhA5yQ7HPPtK0_UL2b_-2PhS6P1dPAxFKUSnqmLgPX3sPbFy246JgRk64BC-kA_heFZr5mSVZktJMjIgz_5VuCawOS2SEbr_BENEd6eOUrBg==> .

 

The Year Of Mobile

 

Mobile ad spend continues to take a larger portion of the spend pie, and according to eMarketer it will account for 22.5% of all digital ad investments. Google is in the No. 1 spot in terms of ad spend, but Facebook has ascended to the second spot now that it has opened up its news feed inventory to include mobile. Mobile apps aren't the whole story, as mobile Internet spending is expected to grow 105.9% to top $18.15 billion this year. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001GseQtw40XEJnokXSFi9DVORgAuGYsRJ2VT5UpdEroOyW8W0YphPAyz-W653Fl3SoxGrTznON5lVKJJoe4n1g64bJbeiFD5b10jU-XuQT24uaA8VodAXAFxP3AiEX4oBE7Q8OybWJrD6p6QavnihDjy4dIFAOW5gUU0omiup8eTSIpwIO4ALDfzd9PTu4C5TdIO9EIWDnS_Wxen1Ze7b-m-pc9Dk3eYp1XRpGByEnojU=> .

 

Photo Ad Case Studies

 

Instagram took a stab at monetization by offering ads on its platform and so far the company is happy with the results. A blog post details the results of two companies, Levi's and Ben & Jerry's, which both used in-stream ads to engage with fans. Levi's was able to reach 7.4 million people in the United States over nine days, and Ben & Jerry's reached 9.8 million over eight days. Instagram reported a 32-point incremental lift in ad recall. Read the Instagram Biz Tumblr post <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001GseQtw40XEJgpA9vAoH2Xdz7XR_HgPsOvkR-faoRQirQVGLnFe_HtqtR_0el2oAyevQPFVM2TdpA87yMFT6Ku5vpfMdxhSofeytpL8hjYGUD4q-zXQVSurSrfOZG5_XoNafE74bRL3Q0blk4HxWNS6ukzwXVXaNAsq30LcN0S4_fuhFgovNgZo4-yvXKMBf9DzFhgYqyZMGN-byTk9WWtHRfMFznagWv> .

The eBay, Amazon Battle

 

eBay's 34 acquisitions in the last five years (and recent unification of many of them under the eBay Enterprise umbrella) have prepped it for a serious fight against Amazon, according to Jeff Himmelman of The New York Times. With the majority of commerce still occurring offline, both retail stalwarts are racing to connect their own respective worlds of digital wallets and Web marketplaces with same-day delivery, marketing services and cross-platform identity plays. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001GseQtw40XEKve0c6pUKmq4wLm80C0YMmy-4ckZTvbeqoLIVIo0tAlqCOEQVnhvKV5Zz-F0IPUMnBUh8lqJ3ux4ATLSJEGUG8mxSq4zl0d9t7rp6W3LorbqIWSHZhrMdjABTEzPW1ntCqU6eWsopePac0J9US04YI_F6lskilQyClKthBY2tp1Sff87V1bPNEDWXzI8mLN7OS6YnDkI-RL5x2-xMEJs7W5a3N5PhQTtsodQxEqh-_4x33323DOGFUygxVvgKuFpe5DJgZgNWlAw==> .

 

Bots Are Winning

 

The topic of impression fraud has been pretty hot this year, but as Solve Media's quarterly look at the problems shows, the problem is as intractable as ever. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001GseQtw40XEIzKA7G_GOdwDAVmrLFGj0Rn9dRbY9CnhGMBLpXF9FPVxE3c5xQOzn7JZ9yqSp7MX4jrzh5I8N_irUJaGg52sHwpEn4wK5EIWppPGNnmUqnVdl0vM4Ux3uBSkTmBzwpJCpxqsKBwH6e-X4tQIImc4tUGNxqPc4LA0yljKf9b-Cvag==> . The report found that 51% of US Web activity during Q3 was believed to be fraudulent -- a rise of 8% in Q3 2013. The solution appears to be in the promise of viewability -- another big topic in 2013. "As fraudulent Web traffic in the US rises, marketers must defend their hard-fought budgets by investing with publishers that ensure their branding is being seen by actual people who can truly complete purchases," said Solve Media CEO Ari Jacoby.

Video Fraud

 

Adweek's Mike Shields continues his coverage of fraud issues in online video advertising, this time focusing on video technology company OneScreen. According to the article, the company was working with Touchstorm, which reported a slew of issues they faced before ultimately dropping the company as a vendor. OneScreen has also faced problems with Meredith and HealthiNation, which creates problems with video companies such as Tremor and Videology. "Anywhere we tried it, we couldn't get any legitimate traffic. And we tried everything. It makes me wonder: Is there any real traffic to be bought?" said Touchstorm CEO Alison Provost. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001MoHvhPRqm9sil_t-Wnr8kT2mfHfcXZXblfww0t_wZUBls4nkeRoHPwIAdZyOO8Zdtsmc4IqehEQj1XfqKQ-IZldQQQAdMa4DylIUqPEX9fvl26lUrbl5_B19heJM7qn0EthxCi7eeJC1NLG-ExYcqUe6NCvf5Q8Ia5ma-GByJxNnwkhBKSvEdRT3WSoXiD6VFcojbU59laOt8v31uDM_67nIlJYDeCU7pH-iGDiZudo=> . Adaptive Media acquired OneScreen seven days ago <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001MoHvhPRqm9s5i_RSSYJXs6pdpvkVAN7xvQ7TJxCJXx3ma1NZX4PpRQN-EgynFwQbQjNZ-3KxhfHJmnfBIcKQLLvtIpve1fGM7oO5fNODt_J04fRCEpJgO_zoWfgo_7OQdpAdwfTA2oLbNjomesHjdH365LePfn04hpNOoAO1pW5fISbNza_lNwRHFqWWTFMOBiAmEiWdW83FUpytRZSaSBhLGRD6voMBjKCctnRKZKKDK1Cq6dyZKZxfFZQ5t2SUeH5G4qhO60hYr3K1DI38uw==> .

 

Marketing Acquisition

 

It's not just "big data." Big money is swirling, too. According to The Wall Street Journal, coupon circular company Valassis has agreed to be acquired by Harland Clarke Holdings Corp. for $1.3 billion. Read more (subscription) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001MoHvhPRqm9tSMM3rO4Pce64eRtNXpRhytM-xIXVfSXCVkyD1jyb0IuZC8Jh886K2XIcHzizthsCQdgDIFqrWdkhECTZZMd-t8QS5KqQ12SiyNkVALwapKBZMrWm-UYJl8FL2meD5liwscJByvWWbg-_oXvJCo3CrlA4l8uEna7P2fX9WI44_6ni81ZgezZizm-c3y8FmUos=> . In a note to investors, BMO Capital analyst Dan Salmon sees synergies behind the purchase: "Harland Clark's top verticals include financial services, insurance and government, while Valassis's top clients are in consumer packaged goods, food & beverage, grocery/mass retail/pharmacy, quick-serve restaurants and telecom services." Valassis acquired display ad network Brand.net in 2012 (read a bit more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001MoHvhPRqm9svHQF8G0QgZPoQnIUipQ9IM8fwsIBlUf2r_kVUOnHZbEC4WZlxDbkuksO6YP3JXf7S-X4Zb_PvYhit35JmE6jekut0qBBCkHbCHOuxhKgThONNhfrQPbfbIikHoU214qgvRRaintsIoQSUjKU_cFpto_2ouZM26X32OGrwCMWVmQ==> ) to augment its local digital ad strategy.

 

Social (Ad) Sameness

 

As the social networks start offering similar services they could risk losing creative potential with marketers, making it easy for them to duplicate message across networks. Emerging social media sites may still be innovative from the marketers perspective as they fill niche sharing needs, as Ad Age points out. A comparison chart of the current major social companies shows just how homogenous they are becoming, but it's always up to the user and marketer to make the most of what each site offers. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001MoHvhPRqm9v5NzA5DbPeGreEOKul58XhIHrRcebzYlV2mTye_mjuuUZwa3FEdig4wg6W8GZGIrNN_vnG_xK5v2AgNmNrMt2h8jp8DI3QYpS99skeQc1zSJJvPOi7ebNjPeaFsgNjoOdfump6ICMkfjRcNiNg7IbYNwSRy16V_qi43uJDsZoGv9GZt9YN5eZ-Pyp-ASCQ1xTqRUPcmEDJaeqCWzyJQS7P> .

 

Business Data

 

Audit, tax and advisory firm KPMG is acquiring Link Analytics to apply the power of data to its services. "Data is everywhere, and today's consumers are more informed and discerning regarding products and services, and this has produced a critical need for companies to understand what drives those behaviors," said Alton Adams, a KPMG principal in management consulting and US leader for customer strategy and growth. According to the press release, LinkAnalytics offers "customer experience, large-scale social network analysis and network optimization" for businesses. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001MoHvhPRqm9sJZgvDqqqgIptp7nVhiRQNZIQT4IHKXyaqUbY3zc4iXqIZBjEHHoMgaIcPRB7M8J2naqns1jIJzs5p5EjK7MzfZihHBu-r9rbE8CEGbkQyhCUajRuMolctuMXu0OXCNl_UAG73QUwGyIZTshaiJYGWv5EPfwyUPeA0VLbEwg_JpQSXSB4iX3oaivpTZWYbKKRYm2fxM4A4E8yRQdUOhevmamuPKm1XtmKZM4fsGd0bOGXZ3-3wMVPgH-HWJRpoG6JKYODbEZIwjHnJ6gjskp9v5Ka5eNkD7XKHP3k9Mtk-zGPVNnIQvZ4EXZrdEZtppIE=> .

 

Native Social Surge

 

The latest BIA/Kelsey report found that native social advertising is growing faster than social display. According to the report, native experienced a 77% increase in revenue this year, driven by social. "Display remains the most prevalent form of social advertising throughout our forecast," said Jed Williams, VP for consulting at BIA/Kelsey. "At the same time, native advertising formats are quickly emerging as alternatives to display that can generate better engagement and performance." Adaptive Agencies

 

It's time for 2014 predictions and Digiday is serving one up about agencies. As marketers and brands try to figure out digital marketing, agencies should benefit, according to the article. They have the opportunity to tie their work into hard business metrics and can help manage the confusing array of marketing and advertising technology. "The spectrum of services that agencies can offer is growing," said Rishad Tobaccowala, chief strategy and innovation officer at VivaKi. "The fact that Accenture, IBM consulting and other companies are all aiming at marketing says it's a growth area versus a shrinking industry." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016eZ0cy6PkfywY_8U1E8SaMnU7cLZwbsfEzKlAvSHzzXbt8b8vuEWrRvuWHumkyB6F2wMtHAs9ifLdIG0DqZxLLBpyIR3-82zP2AthVbH5-W3djkPc2KuoAOPLktSjtvrPsSIJQBKnJRDsQyrhTPw8D7vTWdCMM06> .

 

Yahoo Grabs Content Tech

 

Yahoo has acquired content infrastructure play PeerCDN, TechCrunch reports. The company's technology "makes it possible for visitors to sites to do things like chat via text or video while browsing without any additional software." Some see "white space" around publisher tools to support things like holistic yield management and commerce. Could Yahoo make a credible run at it this elusive opportunity? Simpler explanation: This tech will support video on the Yahoo domain with new talent like Katie Couric and David Pogue. More. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016eZ0cy6PkfxEeDdEKuyO5_mFvtq_Xa5QVlqp8dnGBITLiCOAN6h1GgaL6XAvHX-FiFVtbq_GjjlOOS41Z95g4MYcqbtpyizX3wvJAwpdu3e7LdlAT98gE2EXmlmzbHKnTpXpNvvaQHPDUr0VOnYb-BGKX_tDQ_B-rxJRShEQraY=> 

 

Targeting Travelers

 

Sojern has raised a $10 million Series C to support its vision of delivering targeted ads to travelers <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016eZ0cy6PkfyEqRoiAexT5nH0rnKYjsKh7C3Y5k3yyUMH72G-L2jbJFKgToKDMJRpVG4dfOWnq0jJd2GA3lFkS_EoKR9kMo1XGdsXWG29QmJAv8g7d548_2hqio2_sqCu8tZ8ijrWEP0_Lw4eOtUHo9gVrQcvqEaaPIZVHLT6jElCqZyy966EsFxx0cTg1FmITIowP6y0uzYZQe_XKPQWRmNSYm1NRxDJGegplFHa-ahYL8FXcfqLJQ==> , bringing its funding total to $42.5 million. The company will use the money to "aggressively recruit commercial, engineering and data science talent to develop even more granular, self-optimized and intelligent targeting solutions." Understanding customer intent is particularly critical in the travel industry, added CEO Mark Rabe. "With other verticals, lookalike audience modeling is important, but in travel, intent is a much bigger story," Rabe told AdExchanger. "And so we're working on getting even better at predictive analytics." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016eZ0cy6Pkfxmw1jmLzzfBNsw-4b6Uw9p1o-z_Spih8kKRA8pxSX6NhZQ6HQ9slZednK5ejRwMzoJAS0ZPQhpaW6B-ryJ0dfrsRYXCam29eo3K1eQGTYvmgsgAOJdHmGWL6OpVmtDwe8gkTB485_OSBouYQ6IJQH4EtjaNxuS9o-TpjkbALFHa8AvO7W_JC19Wv6Ifgjb5oP2hStwpG3O9a_gnAMWOOXpcmIupT_BAXMNCg14wOwortiLvge4bS6tX68zyP5-AaM=> .

 

Amazonian Transaction

 

Rumor has it Amazon has quietly acquired mobile payments startup GoPago in a bid that pits the commerce giant squarely against Square and, for that matter, eBay and PayPal. As TechCrunch reports, Amazon's mobile payments push has been pretty limited so far - think in-app payments via the Amazon App Store or through third-party APIs selling Amazon products. With the recent launch of Login And Pay With Amazon, digital wallets don't appear to be the only thing Amazon's eyeing. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016eZ0cy6PkfzhvJyoFRkt6cW2_bHJazw020mRbnlnDX_qXYfjdbfMLE3bN4O3re8T8BA2TertP0yekgcLlHvWzO40X-Y5a1IbLo0iXn3vspy5-HaaDvsKtKjMDvP2Uz49LMEEFFoBYCx3_COW59Xzw6GbRQohLa5cnyN_dAis7NGKHLuXkDiJdXovwsbo9fADX_DMK8k8bNOmZ877yUV7ip41XTGEpZs2Q3vavNy5bBtQ4XJ6zs1YkP_KvbO906i48CaM3CHkoUY=> .

 

Data Team

 

JiWire and Datalogix are partnering to bring offline data to mobile advertising. "This partnership ... will increase the effectiveness of mobile ad campaigns by marrying offline spending data with JiWire's robust mobile location data and measurement," said Michael Cohen, SVP for strategy and analysis at DigitasLBi. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016eZ0cy6PkfyOZSLlFlx6ENg007ocXlqmY_e9pY277ydYcacmHDlaLJWR8wRUk2S3xiJqh2y720D-eN0uVQNHxZ1kZoHVSk8h7ea02w3qkdJ2P3CVT3txrmAgHJQlJXzOmLxKo3iR6kGfi3kNGaIq2JodwDJQ-Z4q1P3OS5yi0q3CWt4QcqlI7tdR-nbjS9kEXt55e4jKPoXFSZq70gO-6JYPSJFg1PKtjuoFdO5Hd-hpDHQIUwUCAQEeTwD3kqixLbYOkj-6deQ06vE4o4qKFw==> .

End-Of-Year Reflections

 

As the year draws to a close, Google reflects on changes that have occurred in the advertising industry on its Think Insights blog. According to the infographic, RTB buys experienced 74% growth, and 70% of advertisers and publishers now deploy programmatic. See more (pdf).  <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016eZ0cy6PkfxnrymUMtY2ys_wLsaeRQW96wRAGq8UzDrhF_px-7NB9W3TgA7T39rkASr5PpNn9ZxRbs-SgH6o0hpszj4-p7e4dXuTX6rT2ukGzdCaBNOU2BXgNxQOsnqJBUOYTezjPZarQk8AJhyxltGOFiLCgD_8fAQPFq5ubRsT87_qKu1Odz79IIP1-JyucqnSkKJ4SGE=> And read the post on the DoubleClick Publisher blog <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016eZ0cy6PkfyOTPonMLiHrZViPnPCxVPe5kdsITj5MtSXs188TNfHuHu8kk4fMdMn6hTMpKS2fti4Z_zzXeo-1zNQIFhDDtQgE9uUq5wYKujqDB-hO3ywOgcW-fa3zgAFjuPUUcbuKKC29r3Uv96eMyvghVnl8Cc2ePT1vVi82SJxYXFEpUm5BDMV05bPD7OytOSq3ncI-L50Nx07Q8mskQ==> .

 

Data Hires

 

EXelate announced two hires to expand its operations. Deb Josephs will serve as SVP of global human resources and Matt Bennathan as VP and managing director, UK. "As the demand from marketers and agencies for eXelate's products increases, we sought and found innovative thinkers and industry leaders to join us at the helm during this time of significant company growth," said Mark S. Zagorski, CEO of eXelate. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0016eZ0cy6PkfxFcyjg5jzNx3xUywmZEGCkvsnWXHVM35uyhK8QdasEnPgK5Gce8SAUW9joWHdapKjBCupljvw-Vs8oOXXFSC8qlAaM2ut_6C25kBffW0FmynjFtSzDQkYsLTVsAEWCPRzYzwFnQCxjZoYLDwE4F57_Dvu0LgJdmwxSPT6q1cFXENuKo5dj7tQg5hEH4r8SPCxSTqQ90BZMFB_653qDUDZzBrv7Npa_Ik95cGa3t-GuLm3vwlpA6a8N_ECE1gcSmyaU7gfbSjsLjQ==> .

 News Round-Up <http://ih.constantcontact.com/fs116/1102602719219/img/94.jpg>   

Here's today's AdExchanger news round-up... Want it by email?

The Apple Exchange

 

Apple is pushing its iTunes Radio inventory, according to Adweek, as it aims to compete with other ad-supported radio services. It's also looking to create an RTB exchange for in-app ads. However, sellers are being told to focus on radio right now. "The message that came across was basically if you're not working on iTunes Radio, you're irrelevant," an Apple insider said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJULCQvvCCd7110MHW3qH7UsuxArH5vzLmJEKlrMx8NKnJPrtfqslxPLkgsuibv_6ZlgxhQlYeP9AtWLUHtUn7tBooH97D1p3R_5oDKh4_llzFMhpLhniokJgfS_Dt4hOloCb8yoMisCZlNT-QJaekngDavK4neVmbfJv6iIDXkjPQjPuhfg8i8T23xN7Gddmx4=> . Related: Apple's location tracking initiatives. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJWr23ryzcuF3IW6Pp4Pm0EJNSIk_FUUqqXZaT9Yr2-h_Kl0akXCTt2fkXvSproUgy15xzvGmZMt35ctrFmOXoY1WGn2Z73afZUL1BXKcUlRDWu6PxYL8FHIIxn5W2-1yWQC-LomXlKPLR-BhVdWxJbmT_tAiP360Zd1bliWMgBQAVOquOHKT1wcrrzwMpNggZQ=> 

 

Automation Up

 

Mobile RTB experienced huge growth this year, according to Nexage's Analytics Report, with bid density up 200% and bid volumes growing 500%. Private exchanges are driving a lot of interest in automated mobile buying with companies like Nexage, which said revenue from private exchanges grew 569% in Q3. Read more in MediaPost <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJU3dXJbVCa1H09zRg3foXQKCaiKLCZa9DhkU4dKpvFcEcCsAG_NqQ1QLIxweA1EXAI4n6F0sFESZpgDAyTZqWyg8jwUKXyKYc-RcVZ9i3HkFl2XAgfevfTR9OXOUeFT-epP5VixzdeNEiKw_si_tibg1EEZWJEXw6O8COk0wh7Wz7V8lUMkussC56pgRIBqBp9U92PoE7IJ2HG_rS8fj0Av6dfA3oOl_Yo=> .

 

Not Over 'Til It's Over

 

Tim Armstrong hasn't totally given up on Patch yet, despite massive layoffs and closures of aspects of the hyperlocal news project. In a New York Times profile by David Carr, Armstrong says, "The long-term vision was clear: If you get the consumer, can you get the revenue? And we have a whole bunch of Patches where the answer is yes. But we rolled it out on a national basis and we've had to adjust based on the investor commitments that we have made." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJX4Rqmmw3W2JQMc6AhFTyYeEKftXbARj5lXfqtk_dYSR9e0JgtaY4KXj7Y9nt4d4MHqyoBGU7RtNdynTazhY7ELWS6StI7iM1mbEUdhmvSkGuX8dbyBB-oKvCcZ2UhyOcf_Bul97iZgDgkf2SmYsxVZezrxVDYQ1z5--jWNDwyEkqY5j5jBIcTDj5X0AaaodBuROVPgwRcN72LXYbGnJQs5rwxI5kkLai-6UncW6MKrvg==> .

 

Multicultural Content

 

Latino content-creation network MiT has struck a short-term syndication deal with Univision to feed original and partner-produced content (en Espaol) to its respective digital properties. There is still a gap in supply and demand for digital video content catering to the Hispanic market, according to Charlie Echeverry, MiT's chief revenue officer. Advertisers are interested in video advertising, but there is still a shortage in supply. Distribution deals as such could be an answer to forward-looking monetization opportunities for media companies. Variety has more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJX0VPJAKyr81jVz9wA-IJ8BxcyoD_QYEyDbDFsj5jrBO_lWqn5ZUSUrnlRHXmNJDV0bzZBb-Kbh58wFX-2Mo7yn3B9zCso5pUq-CABQ_6I8XAaPgtwY_hSMjONgKVVnYJpUE67XEExMFu87uf0wwPwwK-42IKpD0jVcifK4sh0MkIJDxYOWq2RKLYiEfMd-pyU-a-jb7NGircSYuzVCleSutMFbkiRWx65ID-hzo-jMt_UVKwrlA4hZ> .

Sly Fox

 

A year-end blog post details adoption of Mozilla's aggressive browser privacy features and its mobile OS. Firefox users have downloaded Lightbeam, a tool to visualize Internet tracking, 1 million times; and 10% of the browser's roughly 550 million users have adopted do-not-track. Additionally, three device makers in 14 countries are supporting the new Firefox OS, and wireless carrier partners are in place. Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJUaab4rywyfJCcmRBpAley8YVgpQL511aIkTtC_w12yDR2pIOFGL3VLlv_ZfMeX83s1sFKCCnSHGIxmxEUiR7ia5f96rIrvueKe5avKnvhHBLL6FLx1LNMVsF0tgba_CSd1yEU7JbREpu7dmY12CyXeY6HcnUFEmotLbG1xb7Fdzg==>  There's no mention here of Firefox's ad-monetization ambitions, but those are real too, as evinced by the recent hire of Darren Herman <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJUwMpXt_Gx6htxwuASMafGoJTmg0Aj6NkTnc4Wqj0WhxeBVbFrcIsu4xwkEQz_EhtOmq-LgN33wTCDFodMXvSW30elk4NUNCqLK8iYXNXTc2FEC9UDd9l7xhmw88xQ4e-Q9vW8_ihlHGQjIyblwzYj2ZjKIbc4S7BO9GEizYESGt0bykrYv2qjDlKpA8Y5tgPM7tPnqkrQHTcGdnMy9XJyGtkGdFoZtBDs=>  to a "content services" role.

 

Defining Programmatic

 

Programmatic is the buzzword of the year, but not everyone knows exactly what it means. Media Life Magazine spoke to Lauren Fisher, an analyst at eMarketer, to try to define the concept. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJXJYrnjF-_c3NQ-gmIYZt4v3Qst935-O7k2dXg2Z9Hi6A0FZ4igoU-QCnZOSZ2yduokTBbsoGknoJIK8x4v5CKAG3gagwGuxcik1rJMMz-fuUeYaB5a8DYrgSjd20Vi3Mo3elMFrCDjL5M_p9MRH2k7UivI6M8STg9KChx5mdU4ou7akcE1GFew> . And read AdExchanger's buy <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJXeQxL9jP3M716gMsfK0NfefTkwZXvPOA9M5U0K_UIv1Fgss7qdRyhYOpPDLItCqkIaR0NppDUtptP04zTobERI-f_udzHn_Ch5nq2LwMfERkGg9wCi4TA0U6IfZivb1fTWJxt5Nsl6Sx5TdvKC4wshjtf4eeGD68bH3A_lbfa9Ko4rWmTwZqKJ>  and sell-side <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJVzgCZRj-omZtsfUP-0GDShm7D8UxLCxcrj_QxuO-eyrpp4LynTVhA4ssRoN2cdhoNgPZjHwHivo9jtgqGEjpFR44_mDWPcZvEldHvS1FbKI2QD6a92uoXA1QC_MZNWdFpG3xoJuhVY5BiUeCECDxM5kxwWSFwu5a2fiN1DUjw13Q==>  definitions from last year.

 

Google Goes After Brands

 

Google has its eye on brand advertising dollars through a YouTube lens, according to USA Today. As the content on the video platform improves, especially in terms of brand safety, CPMs are steadily raising. Some companies are even committing to upfront deals with Google for inventory across different products, including Google+. "We work with a lot of TV-friendly brands and our activities have grown exponentially with them on YouTube in the past three years," said David Cohen, chief investment officer at MAGNA Global. "More than 100%." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJWBOVId4655WIOwFwQzL2CfA9mNIkoXCB21403vjEGtRqeW-Cc7_BSTuiBOiNboksh_EmY2u1ZnYzSreyRl63bUYuGxBkLIKM0G-w7dQunMUpNFhBUqzefo1bv8rKF6YkDl0oNPQluDgyF306qpK-L6LmR7hAOuwJdXLZaBrgnL9bZsLgjLq9Nmeruwuq8qFNisez_5v6_QJZinQK7Oo89K> .

 

Tablet Lag

 

New research from StatCounter revealed that tablet usage is lagging behind mobile (phones! - in this case), and is not growing as rapidly as it may seem. "The perception is that tablets are proliferating and replacing traditional PC and laptop machines so we developed our research platform to isolate tablet usage stats," said StatCounter's Aodhan Cullen in prepared remarks. "In reality we found that tablet Internet usage globally, at less than 5%, is still relatively small compared to desktop and mobile." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001HvwgHaAWQJVrvJ9aZKfo86ijS6SHUN5ek7PCwgFOHze8UCbFo5A-eTnj7uuZUpO_u_ClNuLB0dMiU6XpCD4g_VQfsUiR5edEZtST_05joD-ISLZJbi0W8T51qx0iDcBBx5bEgDCSWYdvDFyQscAeIR9GHYOtOT7KGjJKfSjMqZwlF2WpcaaikwgM5M-IVptGMXhLaoDjhds3pdpCGMsgPnfeByYMel5jywnWka-Q2XICrphnsF3MlA==> .

Custom Buy

 

Marketo purchased Israel-based Insightera for $20 million, according to GigaOM, giving Marketo a website customization platform. Insightera uses visitor data to tailor a website experience for each individual in the hopes of making them more receptive to ads. The company is a competitor of Demandbase, with which Marketo has a partnership. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00125d7_T01vjc4uXkGUBjLzSnGsnCg_2vmIFL2o6yRarr06BoSwMHF9rNrNTE2fF_jsm8Z8NDH3y1-MGMW9GS-8HHEgfpMjyfsmO4lSSFTx3C5o9kPYOmCksE9N653PS7YTByG0bWhdu2z_bg_onaNqpJhGwAPt8AtWK7v1lwr9yumEE-uYceY4luyPvIU8_q_n4figEtPg3rP96Wi_w1fcRmXOWb7ORYOPj3Fz7y94B902QfUMGNWMgE0BtqDBm5e> . Ohh, it's a tangled web the ecosystem weaves.

 

New News Publishers

 

Last Friday, the FT reviewed UK news "upstarts" and the advertising challenges that may lie ahead. Trinity Mirror has launched UsVsTh3m in attempt to do battle with Daily Mail's MailOnline. So far, UsVsTh3m has no advertising, but 7 million users per month after launching earlier this year. Carla Buzasi, editor in chief of the Huffington Post UK, tells the FT, "You can go from a standing start to being an established player in the British media scene." Read it (subscription) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00125d7_T01vjfVtxe5yhCBcs8IiucZUTJDddBtWQd2F0bP_KNozGmOZu2PcYZeTyX_d5Wgo_P3XSzhBq8HMSYpMbrVjckUFfGo1oRaQQSWpdqkJNid-LYroS3JlNefmRwzPxDX5veDf9gTseqHYXBst9Q0QOWpwK_TgiO0MkevqKXfVk8EqRfIHp0WWlCC93QL> .

 

Email Changes

 

Google's changes to Gmail that will automatically display images have some people wondering whether the move will be bad for marketers. The ReadWrite has collected a few cons, which include the inability to use images for tracking multiple email opens and breakdown of geolocation data. However, with images automatically displayed, users may be more receptive to marketing messages. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00125d7_T01vjczYrZ8ezdD4j6sKvEgwgS5O5LExJfWycZyHHEnaY53TC9BXgkk3TWVC0I6IX-NhArByb2HBscEWWkoGuFQiuWw_0pldC0kGSgpUF52Edivqdv12HlpXKU8uswxZ9KOwKtwXqFBvOkU-8KeM_9h_WzTvAI2ZcOgqwmFBLccOYT5r8GwpACnglFNTC2zrSrzkK-zuhhsDp2sLg==> .

 

Fraud Uncovered

 

According to Business Insider, a Telemetry document reveals that a large British packaged-goods company lost $488,000 of its video ad budget to fraud. After the traffic data was decrypted, Telemetry discovered that a lot of it was coming from Asian porn sites and no-name search engines. The unidentified ad network was subsequently dropped, but it isn't the only advertiser to fall victim to fraud. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=00125d7_T01vjcXOKKx-lvgvYz4nvaOi7rrjE6x6nrDKb8nLxzy4PbEfjkxAlLZasx18n393bXcTXplS2j_F6-vunLL80cSLNUaT72nH1dbB5SZE1AbBmc-_gi2RAL7ab0Y4TTRx-HWLmU9uGJmTInCrbl5yoCJ5C7BFqlyZRlZGVS7t4vlexiwpUJt1KcOTeW7> .

 

Facebook On Video

 

Facebook has better reach the TV, better targeting capabilities than YouTube - and potent video ad measurement tools coming out in Q1 2014 which could give it the definitive edge. So says a "leaked" document for buy-side partners, obtained by TechCrunch's Joshua Constine. Constine opines, "It may not be the platform with the biggest reach, targeting or engagement that captures the ad dollars fleeing television in print, but the one that can best prove its ads actually work." Speaking Of Measurement

 

Facebook is bringing offline data to its Custom Audience product - marketers won't have to go to Facebook-approved vendors to make this happen anymore. Part of the process is explained thusly: "Marketers upload hashed data, including emails, phone numbers and addresses, as well as encrypted transaction information; Facebook matches the retailer's hashed data to hashed data from our own databases..." And then, and then... "Will Be Tracked For Discount"

 

AT&T is willing to trade tracking privileges for service discounts, according to Forbes, as it brings its Google Fiber-like service to Austin, Texas. Users get a 30% discount for allowing AT&T to track them through "AT&T Internet Preferences." Here's how they present this offer to customers: "If you are exploring a new home appliance at one retailer, you may be presented with similar appliance options from other retailers. You might receive these offers or ads online, via email or through direct mail." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LSEefSShJ5iru6BTH72PK3qZ-aZKDGWJb4CUXgRZBZ8lDpsdNL746Zw3J3MBTv0vv1xmvp8jAlxvK7yfkgpGJF8mNtpSZYs32K5abcScMczLDzFC37vf02TUZhJ6DoElzSoyyhjZCMJE9ddipswowqNynSseGgwDTH1bz1KFDxfurB3uqWmV03bQwkOb8DVrwdDYCl833wsLxHkc2n0PD0oZi7kT2bdyqXVuuJBHMeAHvCmt9YLOoplMLhaJAfoJx2ilpRVNVzQ=> .

 

Retargeting Profit

 

Ecommerce retargeter TellApart is profitable and growing, according to a video interview on TechCrunch. CEO and co-founder Josh McFarland lets a few numbers out of the bag, saying his company has a run rate of $100 million per year. Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LSEefSShJ5hhE_5dviWkmus2Vm9OuLTjwv2JVRpZC46TZs64HcwSXNmuuHURaKIHRiFj_0KKcBwYwf0zUoa-SDkSzss9UGUn-7GSoU3rLW0b3XpwgYYY3a3PL5frR7B_YKdLGVSOZEZ1bdapVM8W-i43Bz_geQIDiKr6NAB3dWRAcJ4SY6vpTSoC2xM13Ja_lpWMNvrNswleaiZkyf6h5BYmflIZx89Z> . TechCrunch points out the company has not taken any funding in two years. TellApart's competitive set includes the now-public <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LSEefSShJ5gctkOK_q4dCKY3rTOcAv3Xm9P2Z60qKtgp93NW4NQ7Qcg9BMTGfKtOS9ws6NhMBQY82PxpkfTOFqX95IYW1wYdI1KoRR-4zLKTV3MWkSLQN-vQrM1oJ-iHSRb6Y2h7Irvqw2qiomAkQvKt0eRjUK2ykf7GVGuh2cENcJXerSgW3ASX2lFCjT6t>  Criteo and ValueClick's Dotomi unit <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LSEefSShJ5jwcYwzMSnb7hf5EnOxreTJbuUe_IlsO0oNpJBbQYJAk_WypQRmsOSL-lpshUHCjzxee3Q2JTkqFsarTi8el84SyRzrWBfvw_JkGdZ25clUkupBZX3VlMECY1xsA3Phpl7RgW4ji0DRqPkKKt4ztcmD9f4sWA77E7FHnTVJM32BIsfy4b4Opm0eiAUzj3PiT5H7oBobbcFpLg==> .

 

Surveying Retargeting

 

Marketing Land and Survey Monkey partnered on a 400-person survey about consumers' awareness of retargeting. One question asked: "How concerned are you that retailers can show you ads for their products after you have visited their websites?" The results: "Very concerned 18.87%; Somewhat concerned 34.80%; Neither concerned, nor unconcerned 29.4%; Somewhat unconcerned 6.86%; Very unconcerned 10.05%." These are always hard surveys to do depending on how you ask the questions, but some interesting results. Read 'em <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LSEefSShJ5httPNC4lqnskSLu8QZIebDy72tnOeFS_wtN8o3oemWx75GfjDlweIvc8fefyVAbAns1yIjK1Bcu9il9Zk2SGlzYqv446qw0j-AcSeOh-n9mFX9tpuKN5KsyyNIropJZRX-fz38tHEZPfL_1d1Huf_wRkl6UGRCdTBuJyqySjkc1g==> .

Paparo's predictive powers proved presciently potent in 2013. What's he thinking about in 2014? Video Accountability

 

BrightRoll announced a strategic agreement through which it will integrate Nielsen Online Campaign Ratings into the BrightRoll console, a UI for "planning, executing and optimizing digital video advertising." The OCR package measures viewer exposure to ad campaigns across screens. Charting Video

 

Forrester Research spent five years tracking online video and finally published two reports, according to a blog post, one focusing on the US and Canada, and the other on Europe. Among the positives, publishers are innovative, creative and focused on experiences that work for consumers and advertisers. The negatives are mostly on the advertiser side and include such things as a lack of understanding of the nuances of online audiences and too much repetition of the same ad. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LSEefSShJ5ho2YYxKgCc98N9MqnLbRm_wNajgoXEABAkj6BQ1nCg6mimJhYJLJE7GQCtmF-je1kX_1woNDzQMUP_UA78gz4xhmIuEqUKkcsX5qHgYIcEOiLPuM935IDWfGv_zZ8dGko7M8FHgB_UHfJUqfahoXiYVtRwIjTMhsCzfvbfLRUAHmfPiRCIWUkLKeogfQkANJy5msXhwke8AoTJpGDjMT1bksnxXvSKdAM=> .

 

TV Shift

 

The push and pull continues over the value of a time-shifted TV ad, AdAge reporter Jeanine Poggi notes in covering the UBS media and communications conference. Network CEOs have resisted discounts for ads time-shifted more than three days, as some advertisers want. They prefer a seven-day window. "What's the difference if you watch it in five days or six days from now, versus three days from now?" said CBS CEO Les Moonves. Also: The US TV ad market is soft this quarter. Ad Age story. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LSEefSShJ5jgcXJX5xNLjL0pIaQkIZQ7njlpU_hYrLGdjlndnHgQRNepUSlq0nQoS3_8jdU567ZJoJlHPz6leDfYe0TrZYVnjdyouxtMJJf96YRjVPRWEbmhbXnPwxC6l3LGI4HhQsiQeT-dVRFsqM2ciRJlKua6guy_d2Cgc0CkXuShYul114-oClX5ZAClorxQozwLqiQGNb-qRPEgMg==> 

 

Shopping Funds

 

Shopify has raised $100 million, bringing its valuation to $1 billion, according to The New York Times. The ecommerce company represents 80,000 stores, most on behalf of small businesses, but its vision for the future is much larger. "We want to go from being an ecommerce company to a commerce company," said Harley Finkelstein, Shopify's chief platform officer. "That's the vision. Sell anything, anywhere, anytime." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LSEefSShJ5huKb33F6hMUU1bI5l3cxTxJS6qtw8tj3UoDkE3vvEXRCY_QPAP_69aFlyH2WwOBaoBGyWanP93vgjBckXtfH7_8Cayy4Cb1--5Wt1yV3mTzFI80eEVNCkaEohhsCgHJ5jZBT_U_YVIqPtl7FjdHQocnOJ7Vctrb4d9TEjBQwafP0UzcYu_XWMYk4MQK9fgQfosSjCUmLI70EVtIJsa45Kq> .

Selling Sales

 

For publishers who are still stuck trying to figure out how to build a programmatic sales system, the IAB has released a document briefly outlining different stages of the process. The paper breaks down the sales building process into three steps. The IAB also stresses the fact that people need not fear losing their jobs to machines, as there is still the need for the human element. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DRlTpampRYBx-qF0qUWpX37hbueIZDyhQ-ofhNZOj97CCuVSTW1PLhffIrp_qG33_RF_vR1WY4m0X6NcnPIiYRkOF5fU-HMT-R1syK6-BWTeD6dtnxvnVnpRfkL-ZoeUQhOewgCMDK_bwgb6LqY-qq87HLqe0UXHlBvpcJq4Zq00uVt41kGVs9hZRebsezWhYcLHjVhox6o=>  (pdf).

 

Agency Gardening

 

Publicis says it is weeding out some inefficiencies ahead of its merger with Omnicom by streamlining its US and Canada operations, placing them both under the Publicis North America umbrella. A shifting around of key executives will also occur as Publicis combines its operations, according to Ad Age. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DRlTpampRYBCbKmgug7dHzVodEdFZGWSq3HH7mMbyTGqj_aw4ApegyLntDQ3tWnvxW6vMMwt_W2rdHKE4LQW6dsdq8hq4-riuLxaAGGeWJ0AuAFUP3mbcTzT40MDzT-56-L2ItxMe_x5jHjxt1EaOaRL-r0WHYaa9IOZ-8XCJ5wBlUWgpZlbph8ToiDhNGxsktNWPNMVwR6debP4dU69HKR80plaHPL0> . Together, Publicis and Omnicom hope to cut costs by $500 million in five years.

 

Ad Lag

 

Publishers may be embracing mobile video as another way to get content in front of users, but ad companies aren't catching up as quickly, according to Digiday. "The future of creative is smaller stuff," said Ian Schafer, CEO of Deep Focus. "But culturally, that's not the way a lot of agencies work." An example of video ads gone wrong would be placing two 45-second prerolls in front of a two-minute clip. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DRlTpampRYCBOlXNhFBiIU0eoSi9iGCwtInoUKc9XLBsDNCjvm02Fd0A_K7UxNRV4lY1p6b0U-ck1KUmnTou6cHm9RH9otuoQ4Je775RMA7yDaeMFly_9EMVD-ZwJjN21R2TXKdmhYcby7ajB-Dk5AAtMd83rAQXaU5drn3ClaM7bRlHvh6YXw==> .

 

Anti-IPO

 

Despite the trend of video company IPOs, IP-based video firm Ooyala is going to hold out and take in $43 million in funding from Australian telco Telstra instead, according to AllThingsD. "I wanted to be able to go public when it's the right time to, instead of having to," said CEO Jay Fulcher. Ooyala's roster includes ESPN, Bloomberg and Comedy Central. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DRlTpampRYC6qFJFjcORL3OJqcJQtmqRMPk12xp0qsPSsGMmI4DoPlr9sJZ3tcxGS7WSTkmsxZbiODwm29-uc5yhMOlgZSmcbXLk38WmjSBGVnjPuyiP4Tx9-GYrSk0NT4yZ-tsaplJxMv5gk4R8CSED8EEaWkntJYIg1rKY2Uj10dgnipwpQZCBnRIgzAj6> . Convergence lurks.

 

Acqui-Strategy

 

Marissa Mayer's small startup acquisition spree as CEO of Yahoo has gained the company considerable press, which is likely part of the strategy -- but there are methods behind the madness, says Wired. The most obvious is a desire to improve its mobile position and cultivate new talent, but there could be underlying motivations like building small teams that compete internally and produce solutions for Yahoo. Larger acquisitions, such as Tumblr, have Mayer publicly saying she will encourage autonomy, too. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001DRlTpampRYBrnvzAaISIkXwbSEkeRQ5mEGee2RrB4ipQM4IvABnGOCu1WPYfWg7OTIvkYABsGTMFVqGOFUKQqBm1Jc1u5_dxxaiB_hOYN87KTzogBmXut6dOq7nMb8rEIblJKQUJVdIbHS055UpYR9iS3uzrCTeMvlLgR8kBPS07Bk4ImfzoFcd8wu2YK_DG> . It's another way of potentially shaking remaining Y! cobwebs.

Not Gone 'Soft

 

The tea leaves at Microsoft might suggest a move away from advertising (Atlas divestiture, IE's tough cookie stance, aQuantive write-down). Au contraire, writes display ad GM Greg Nelson in a blog post. "Our digital advertising business has never been more important to the company, more integral to our future, than it is today." The vision now is around creating value in the mobile ecosystem. Video Share

The company is expected to net $1.96 billion, which is a 65.5% increase from last year, pushing its global ad market share above Twitter, AOL and Amazon. Tremor Building Programmatic Team

 

Some of the team behind Velti's Mobclix mobile exchange (which ceased <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LpvohpImSDvYdhBCArR6qlUU4JiDHHw_9DsHixBTz3C9WddL-M2jjOsuofgVacfqdRnbV7KmlZXX8BhAf0ucvTV7kqEKu5iephsxf4ZZP7r5jXCe1kCUmXFhUXuGC5ZezGRVJApP7jifA-lkaYDl5AG5Tgxl8LUTJCLUiO7a7MY=>  all operations in November) are heading for Tremor Video, the company announced. "Solving programmatic buying for brand health and aligning buyers and sellers on brand metrics are core to our mission of bringing the certainty of science to the art of brand marketing," said Steven Lee, CTO at Tremor Video. "We jumped at the chance to add a talented team of technology veterans with experience working together on board." Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LpvohpImSDvx3QqdmCJ6VbywWHD6tp4PnctpM2tqVO6yaQsecR4X3DtU3u8bSOLkVdUlVH_1ePSegCkXEYYQI3Ic39K07H_Q2RKk8IX4s9HbNHV3RotJ9opulEZ6N-s96ZNduuiJJxsr-SKtirB0J873QiuAxSu2d2SVK6XaMs4oWHw8xuPe476NaPfMN7rVUKHDk9wpqlTmuZxlDiEeABYntwVIhp3DRMnXXKMnrTrvvaG682ngDA==> . Tremor needs to make a tech and engineering story (mobile, too), not just an ad network story.

 

Disqus Native Ads

 

No place on the Internet is safe from native advertising. Disqus is testing a sponsored comment unit, according to Digiday, allowing brands to put a message beneath relevant articles. Targeting by vertical is currently the only option for advertisers, although Disqus is working on making them targetable at the user or audience level. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LpvohpImSDtYC7UuceRC8gZGUxykeP3RRQMfxQhngH_PbenY5atNJp-4e9XXSmLAAJ4rrixp8IrpGk7kqzml8RaR8DsZ9Ks4oNVZR8D7O3tF0DLgPlzE-Oyj83HazgcUtOVlpxv1I48NEr04wI2ehWCA0GXNRsW-NGwF5ljJ1oUaO01luchuIw==> .

 

Simulmedia Does Too

 

Simulmedia snapped up a cool $25 million in Series D funding led by new investor Valiant Capital. Simulmedia positions its solutions as designed to enable targeted television advertising, bringing online practices to the broadcast arena. Company CEO and founder Dave Morgan (Real Media, Tacoda, more) stated the company will use the new funds to build out its technology, services and sales team. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LpvohpImSDslbWko8imSvhDhMLWkDFLaSltRxXMZY4b4OmjKa9vQilAGPC2W-yMZEPGHr0QDK89EJ-b3py126TgQqeBsfGKKegfM5tubdXMMWLgybZdiVE8r5d9doF5yhyEv7cqmmnxLW-_yU5WtIWRvXgX4yszydrcXY4nuX15fGPiAOqkdKtToSNPSBzL4kDpO1aBTkx-Wk_VWhjsBk3duZuT0OtlL-kFX2rdXXS2vC7mj9OgGXA==> .

 

Big Mobile

 

Mobile is growing rapidly, and according to Zenith CEO Steve King it will be the fourth largest medium by 2016. What's unique about mobile - claims King - is that it doesn't cannibalize other forms of media. "Television is going to continue to be very strong; digital is going to be an accelerator and an amplifier to that," King said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LpvohpImSDtuEO3b6Uu9UVXP_UT4l3rmWqZEQNJuMKReuBpCtCY9jDuqFHtyGijzvLFPsBudoWnG5MM0COJKIZhA6VO-q8ZJp7787r9FO0hhFZHoUNgzGQGRVc6hWN0XOQDlEuFJCQpd84USnZ8Gq2TKWKhrADwmrygHzr4ZO1BNc3NJ4NDMqaJuFs-wxqiqgVP-Tu1s8TshT1yi_atkWLfSsJhe6-dntTbiXS4BBUg=> . Hmmm...mobile may not be a cannibal, but it is a freight train <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LpvohpImSDvh-gLuQqA1rv9RaJDLTRL7PpD72MvapwrmKHSY_U3b2Br4WhcVN27b6BAypidK3cEU5fXYsoiH7dw0Q2Ld2YBeSxW4_C1hPwinh1Aui8B41xCVhE4016AeDLYAn1brwTFUR4WFOwweHgMt-7wRE7WF-V_1USKz_PzsFr0VC1a1V8QFyj_mrSUY> .

 

Transparency Of Sales

 

Securites and Exchange Commission (SEC) accounting branch chief Patrick Gilmore has been none too pleased with the transparency of Yahoo's recent financial reports to the public. He wanted more info on the company's search - the Microsoft deal - and display revenues. In fact, he wrote a letter (PDF) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LpvohpImSDtqoY9S8FCNwPknr7Me2SLpnknlkfdRSbtO-l-IBYDBIXkuG8HoLx4CY_C6GzfSicXOCxrAiZf3SMpFd3W2GGM3tdaycN3jns77TfwPxf4XlQNLoDnNsPwxc3o9lvgsCcJSYcmfLXHdrs5P-b-JFmAaV9g-x9QVpcBuGrhUfXXRc0FXVBabz7q3qhw5Mafbokc=>  explaining his issue to Yahoo CEO Marissa Mayer last September. Bloomberg reports that Yahoo has provided numbers <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LpvohpImSDuyJN5lyGdcD8eCASwWyA86Q7972zSbD8MHZi2kn-J8BkrFRLBX8ug8A6q-6YkIi2oCCnYA3DFMs8swpLQlESF1beKboR1bgaw5eFGzinViKF5JAwhNOJVteWWlbOjMGbGkyfvpwdM2lqRo98cSbvsgSe3hN2DIdk4gBO0_JkhCDoYRjPx539HGDJWx5G9XQXc=>  (SEC). Talent Scoop

 

Yahoo's acquisition of tiny startups continues with QuikIO, an acquihire. The startup originally focused on sharing media between devices, but, according to PandoDaily, there's no evidence that Yahoo plans to keep the technology. Three employees from QuikIO will join Yahoo's Sunnyvale offices, where they will likely use their video and mobile expertise. PaeDae Gets Paid

 

PaeDae secured $11.6 million to expand its ad business, which is centered around rewards. "In order to continue to meet demand for quality mobile ads from the advertiser and developer communities, we must extend our reach beyond rewards and into other forms of premium advertising," PaeDae founder and CEO Rob Emrich tells VentureBeat. "Our user-centric model will enable us to apply the attributes of reward-based advertising to new mediums." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001LpvohpImSDsZcmCAlnQunTKcWTNgogE7ZlPhfEDCEdFDF8wkVOEBg5JYB_ExxvN33ZMt__Z2vh-jgcCh5EnYHYGMsF0Op363781HM7-rdmFzSzh_jIw1ZyrWhiCX1KM9xRxowmlpVBKQkCdqEkRTnKoeRinUJRVlWfGKIKio2wDmht0r6T4cfAx-bByTR1IoKKbE0zcCEKSICSsYJURTb6GB1Zo7osrP> .

Google Pilots New Ad Format

 

According to a post by Eran Arkin <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001QETFmxamSf51Sgg97udabfdoJ-uX4ma-R9R_BDfiTMCZnb2gWdQRlxa5hbfH95T_r5de3caWixNUj04xOK-hh2C0eR26ZWAcmJShLDe5gvoNrSld5BI0bjcx_dJtVaacAyZ7l1pDxI9NcCrMz1IHx71LosOPNlZqBMdsmsaI_NE=> , product manager at Google, the company is testing a new ad format, called +Post ads, that allows brands to promote Google+ posts across the Google Display Network. An example would be using Hangouts on Air as mastheads on YouTube. The ads are interactive by default (i.e., commenting and sharing is a default feature of all the ads, though users must be logged into Google+ to interact or to see comments and shares), can leverage all of Google's standard display targeting capabilities and are cross-device. The ad format, which Arkin writes will be opened over the next few months to more advertisers, can be purchased via an AdWords auction, on a cost-per-engagement basis. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001QETFmxamSf6lIN65nBVl1LOyRIy-EphY9uF6XAc1RL10WtxceAKVjIFc7puiT36rNTzqn6iCjSY0KJXWAA1dgI1RwcZyv1pV2FeJ8yvSE7a-xdgzJ46csSb-5mJThnnGWkROpJpGPiTviO1e5rRVbzAeFjr7ZhUL> .

 

In-Store Addressability

 

The Wall Street Journal looks at how technology is being used to personalize merchandising - and maximize yield - in-store. One example: "Prism Skylabs combines video from security cameras with software to build flow charts of people's movements and uses heat maps to show which products get picked up more frequently than others." Read more (subscription) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001QETFmxamSf6kDkovUhcm0mHg9V7r6qSmrMxK6077roYuQAkUFyuGSDTYTg4EHvigwPim8m0l1m7Z2mUeL8HWkFmAaZwPeWmR6B99BpI8WEU38KpmcmqUegVyb8bEOyuXZTjhxd1MaP-RWSPHN5K7DLoG4z88brbYSOGBMAM55eL8MpQy8ClIUcjS-nEslAblrTGVUgaGTlQ=> .

 

The Quality Of Merciful Data

 

Site Scout's Ratko Vidakovic provides "5 Ways To Evaluate The Quality Of Audience Data" in an op-ed on Marketing Land. He begins, "My aim is to provide a simple framework for evaluating the quality of any particular source of audience data. To do so requires looking at the data from a variety of perspectives: Where did it come from? What mechanism does it rely on? How was it collected? How fresh is it? How much does it cost? And how does it perform?" Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001QETFmxamSf5Qwkz1TVG2V-1s_zlIZ9GzaXlvy6rgUUiGXwPiFWaAB4FU8p2-nTc_btR6Ox_xkS7kDXAZxgOjH4x_16FwA3_kFe7akzFWFSaXpcXPOAPwOOOeHKE7v-BX-Nn65VpC9NxvCaJS6srshhru-M7TcG7ThcbFTruyUTFpt5NmeDHNVG2_T47EHVew> .

 

Impulse Ads

 

Social marketing tech company Getonic <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001QETFmxamSf7s48XxS0-GYmYmN-Uf2HDCAaIibNOx058YtmGUfZmvJ9_WocQ5ub0bzC0h9ZvP9IlEF5atRIvJs_mb9Pn6-5t-5g8M4PfZ_-SDvWQet5aqyA==>  hopes to entice consumers to impulse shop directly from ads with a new format it's currently testing, according to The Next Web. Right now, ads direct users to PayPal to complete transactions, but the company is making the ads completely shoppable in the next few weeks. The ad format is part of Getonic's POPshop platform that also makes use of the social aspect of shopping. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001QETFmxamSf4HqyYcWEJ__6DnKxU3hIXuERISljJl0PBKsEl-j9aMvihMj9Y3CShG5HUP7LkgkGk3aRC2MF9yIako6a3HgGOgqEuEmXHfYGwNCM5w1LbyFVBs4SuBoKhYyVezl4aS19zZVZTvK1rgaoFZ9pcwLGMN_f2lE1h0D60oocHZtVMRAdSElC-Ibfca6ps-z_HkLeErEdid3m0BtsnWcpEyqDLE0-MAEHep9lfVy8Ut_n8wjSvVI7J6l_3u> .

 

Keyword "Programmatic"

 

Adaptive Medias, which bills itself as "programmatic audience and content monetization provider," says it has acquired a real-time bidding (RTB) platform called Ember, according to a press release. Perennial IPO

 

The initial public offering (IPO) cavalcade is not over for digital marketing tech. Ad marketplace Rubicon Project is next and has chosen its bankers. Bloomberg notes, "Rocket Fuel Inc.'s successful offering in September <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dJrOAGPNktHfO8TV2Hvk1DjSTriMKDh7ugXRCsKzXUUB0L_aTN_qkiF4iEMV2NELgMg6at3yYYC4cGgq12Q6hju1xsNyI1KJoCI9-NuGUKyFWPJb5G5fjoEuycp1UyjUQeRBGTZENgBtNzHbSzQRNMyGvkkJgPRunF-eGYpWeem_3EurHfDn85Ets1V7fIB0G7wqE4ZiuCPNMZp8VrUH9Lt>  and the rally that followed Twitter's IPO last month have instilled a renewed level of confidence. TubeMogul ... is also planning an IPO for next year, people with knowledge of the matter said." Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dIipazaMkUAoQEuzLUVQnRl1ZNnVl1SqfrRtzFI65ABf4TKJSH4JKIo73EUqFr2-YOrvkkVxnq_CGHyaUAwgoY2jzCfTiw9r2fPK1rzNCd0_84Lh2aur7D4p1e1syBeAilkFWqVJ10xvJ8rUQLAg_aa1bpJGBA-Y4peGl9zezMgAehw7wtcKqN5FxNHsogEACYUJAk0CZGzPA==> . A bit more from LA Business Journal <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dIipazaMkUAoQEuzLUVQnRl1ZNnVl1SqfrRtzFI65ABf4TKJSH4JKIo73EUqFr2-YOrvkkVxnq_CGHyaUAwgoY2jzCfTiw9r2fPK1rzNCd0_84Lh2aur7D4p1e1syBeAilkFWqVJ10xvJ8rUQLAg_aa1bpJGBA-Y4peGl9zezMgAehw7wtcKqN5FxNHsogEACYUJAk0CZGzPA==> .

 

Attacking The Bot

 

The IAB is stepping up to help buyers, publishers and networks with detecting and preventing fraud by releasing a best practices document <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dJpqmbsd1A-7ZytmPwsz-L661CB2BQ6QYjYbI9Zcsz1_6YQ9CaPELBdD7EhBgnotXV9yBxIeEbj-BFzJEDBflie2cvk61TlgUXUiD4q7XfSyKKr--sqBYhbkvmD_nS_XcSoTYPslDPZY6UU3vvTfGAvOCKanHBRG0alKLXd3B1yZg==>  (pdf). "There's no magic bullet for eliminating fraudulent traffic, because there's no single method by which criminals exploit the digital advertising system. We've prepared this overview of the issue and a set of best practices to start the industry on a path to root out these corrupt practices," said Tom Phillips, CEO of Dstillery and co-chair of the IAB Traffic of Good Intent Task Force. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dLeyRu68Z_z2IPdG7CJBtFKFNRtSKSgs2ByC9SwL8TkygATlonu5h7I_GOpWJCxy0ut15SC9QvFLEy11L32G7usyXrmqOfMOgiKK9iXNLaEj6bcxLJQaCJp-zJDw_Wxt2eLffi0v7KZeBl97XNJpYGfNzglFcsZbS2rZg6YrGE8JVRmWCn4iA_zgLWwV4eaNqzgLWh_NodEdRXORDjI8SyMxhig8qDHdLs=> . In a post on his Searchblog, Federated Media CEO John Battelle looks at white papers outlining the "bot" challenge for the industry. Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dJqj9gV_WTCk3KFBPWWl0Pm4Q03-YOGANmQ5eQJCg96qkdUgWPfTmFl8zBgImFGTEkX7RQrEKh9elmAXZljPcbI8jUrYDjBdwRLzy38IE3f8S5-_1ZRYoztS23oyPtea7dImMsdLjOPIh8RTdluSY7llhogArqqyZxHgUmuT2zhzZPZpvS2Ylcfc8_1wGdhMeB9pI1hTiwytCUPkEphWMPF> .

 

More Bot Battles

 

In the war on fraud, Microsoft has singled out one particular outfit, dubbed ZeroAccess, by taking legal action, according to The Wall Street Journal. This particular botnet was more sophisticated than others have been and so far Microsoft hasn't found the source. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dJrI4eUh-PCVrVlawW2Lgu5NW9n-Kdl4H-Ar3yMgAGQNzjyDo0MO1yqQ_8cw5yCUZuk9_23KZ6jMXQahJulck6OkUd0G6XwrtDKJ3vESsLvl1t_nBKm67Os7M81GhKkyhDBVjUXhVRkdD-ZVfehmhBlWNE8kxrpQecioDQ9qOEFhLP8blRxSVldetFLP6VW6To=> .

 

Beyond The Check-In

 

Foursquare is bulking up its user intent opportunities by offering recommendations for what to order at restaurants or by pushing special offers without the user having the app open, according to VentureBeat. It's also ramped up the social aspect by providing a feed of what friends are doing nearby, along with recommendations for nearby places. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dLwIk7ZfV5yaZBQxjKSmv_GNoPpA5DFDBQZn1mnJprQJfChe3abCi5CIee_uY8a92e1XkKNN4hVMMHNcSYmpEECjTWoF_chHfFEhFzbZUFxmP_L8AukvroY3tyInzx35vTCa-3oLuioha5XOTUxGwTvqThVJwmbNgSA9km2S1yjzJ9OW3BGffF0DIY7nDGXb24-byz39wIT-OAR3ErJXAHASkOsCL_jokA=> .

 

Competition Investment

 

Google is investing in a mobile ad company that it thinks could help bring its mobile ad performance closer to its desktop ads. According to GigaOM's Mathew Ingram, Google led an $8 million financing round for YieldMo, which uses A/B testing to improve effectiveness and monetization. YieldMo founder Mike Yavonditte's previous startup, Quigo, was acquired by AOL for $361 million in 2007. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dLbnjnYZBUtHr6R6LSafkfwPWzaQr9btQETkgJbLoPC90ed7RFS4NU-7XcUIPIkX36__j12aoiXppsQzzL9lDoElCDhIenIna3dyOZJPSEk-sueJliZUOvwZ6chp2V77y15GlaWYuCngKDnv5EiR1L6jM3KQY2WnhDh2jl9DeSvY3Dg9gO65su6aSbRa8WNk6ZqjLfiEqTklBseOHQ-6qbmTnSgvyh1YZWMdF8f7iGtv_gOLYysT7VzN2rzcSI45gk=> .

Smart Gut

 

CEO Jonah Peretti acknowledges the role data plays in steering the ongoing success story of news media platform BuzzFeed, but doesn't call it the be-all and end-all. "It's good to not always trust your gut, to have some skepticism about it, and to constantly have new data coming in and constantly question what you actually know," Peretti tells Fortune Magazine's Andy Serwer. But don't be a slave to the data - he says that it's important to keep gut-level decision-making as part of the content-building process. "It's dangerous to only follow the numbers. I think there's a lot of overoptimization on the Web." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dJWo-BUj4hx1Q94JroooI58thEsfjAA1njeiOYzk2VTD-TA7Qug61f1pduUivKspip3k0Ky9dZhqjRrKJiLCKTZHgdCKicguM5LFCGMK2ig-uCBVfI3yarR-NrEmZ2Nb5O6DvTAAZ2AXIIxfuia0BFpT6KFq7P8DhttniysppWFKoMh9Q9u5rLsvqPWvwYTJTg=> .

 

Paywall Power

 

Rupert Murdoch's News UK operation appears to be offering hope for paywall strategists everywhere. FT.com says that The Sun has more than 100,000+ monthly digital subscribers paying 2 per week with an estimated annual revenue run rate of 10 million (US $16 milion+) for its news offering. But as FT.com's Robert Cookson notes, "The digital subscriber number remains well below the daily sales figure for The Sun's print edition, which is about 2.1m." Read more (subscription) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001yYQyhZyb5dJRUwUS2S6plOIursNe5PtIT3qLCWSTkpTznZT_djz2882HLIEbcZgBIrJM20pHlDpAOnkTvcp8QECpusX5SLEmDV21pS2O-Puzotb2-QxbcLGq6K7Jjo-s40Zp4Ac5WfJbCSB4DiXa0KKKIJoqKeN47PfqPml_9g6hF3gbmb9XzMiRVfi1M1Md> .

The V-Word

 

Neal Mohan takes to the pages of Ad Age to champion viewability in an op-ed piece. He concludes, "Our brand, agency and publisher partners, like Publicis Groupe's VivaKi, Kellogg's and The Wall Street Journal, have been valuable collaborators in understanding this issue and have helped shape our perspective. We look forward to working with them, and the industry, towards an actionable and transparent viewability currency." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001sGUmN75PH-StLVOm4K2MiEXvHB9a1oYVKa5TRy-VqXtiPD_Y17LiTADXp8Oxb4YnuUBJSKVCMQSfcOGxLGvevGFb8IZ8RYqYVHER3goV_hB4J4BaVSFRCwkRleIRIEwtoDTVFwc-P7OYEnoYrgVyuofFOrBciRsaKUCRiKom9SVbrb7eKPf8EBhtERD53fsalsiataNNMjU=> .

 

Native Warning

 

Hey now. At the FTC's open meeting about native ads, according to Reuters, FTC chair Edith Ramirez said in a speech, "While native advertising may certainly bring some benefits to consumers, it has to be done lawfully. By presenting ads that resemble editorial content, an advertiser risks implying, deceptively, that the information comes from a non-biased source." And that's where the problem may begin. Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001sGUmN75PH-TNH5RehPyK3ipKsOlKmM-noVyurcqqCN9mix_YpEZnTGSUjC1_tyxzgGfFU5nb7_VGuSdHqsi7exma_XY1v3Q3XK-9wDKdxhxyzY-7yG8f3cTKL_CqjfsIkUrbYK4v1srdy-iWfglxxEIMmC91HZBh8ashqMObgN2dsoECTcMLHQCSWamxlXMAKvRmWXH6HGhu4-Nv1FdoPTTEOHGIyXMk> .

 

Richer RTB

 

Honda and eOne are testing VivaKi's new "premium" programmatic offering, which supports rich media through RTB, reports The Drum. "This is to attract 'premium' advertisers, some of whom think this [RTB) space isn't really a route for them," VivaKi's Marco Bertozzi said. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001sGUmN75PH-Q0L-AGX__OviS7aHH5unb9ZzUYmGBzpN1c4DH37GjTNWHuwxMq0BL_x75Vf4X63wU61yuaFBuoZsEEuG1rnw3lhf7xOc-k8ca7A71_n9sQbtN_nN662XTIawBlI2qadnlCigYNGm4uphtmls8xLSsrkT_H3YFo5aQfyelgyz4lK3ecLvg-oF94QbDvBoR2GtHgFzQsJEWgHKThHUHwmCK-5BbkizEx9v1KVd27BGjraw==> . The "premium" part appears to be associated with formats, too: "Advertisers can choose from homepage skins, large formats, rich media and video, with all campaigns optimised against viewability...

 

There's No Crying In Publishing

 

Despite online revenue gains for some publishers, print declines have still left a bitter taste. Harvard Business Review's Sarah Green is having none of it. "Rather than blaming their bad ads, they blame the technology and ask for a discount. That is a challenge for publishers, but let's be clear: The challenge is not fickle consumers, the latest mobile game or that "kids today don't read." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001sGUmN75PH-RTcD29b5soYqTrMPL7KAOEVKSSWQdwynReOy-SU5M1rqzDj20xLPAZYKlxwPS2LtndpYGAYCoLdPvs8-0wKBMOy3Wbi70y1RIYaC7LOQuCq10JCi4vAb5lpmXHdBNIkAXFQVdg62zTZGpbp9Rb4_-3fvscJTHD5JJZuc_9uGPf-D7c7o0uwQVl> . Her adversary here is New York Times media critic David Carr and his "needlessly dismayed" profile of New York Magazine. Read that. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001sGUmN75PH-ROvwYz4JBQPRzOX4JIb7E6h1S0xu1_Cs2xVpt8bFCjCw_FGUu7bXgwf0v18TxEWeVaNEl5P1idCa_WSEVVXZNceCkTUpq6Jg6JtFOZ3VeLM-QeXB9ywfz9eYsW7jHN1cdFEEQLWLegPRJJ8EgdpvzNryWkBt-5_CN9uhjKdsqRytkks-WSKQSSqlxmGUiqPG-0FcLl9kMQdjXfORU8U6P7VYqZDbSnNtlBCrtN3u4_pA==> 

 

Go Champ

 

With a rumored IPO on the horizon for 2014, TubeMogul announced <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001sGUmN75PH-Se4CIGd6OR_mP_eKhF7-33KqZskdUNwvXKxcCVlG0xHCbKIipsWJzendm19WEBom2wI_uTkhEbwJKzb5sbmOKnsh23M4ZScS5qRARYcEgy5ntEOXya5Gcl8cine-luvqk-hRwg0Edvo1NkneKVIltZHXafZsSW2izRkWAApLDM1KduuEO4ufbXOCnZavWwnL4hcbN0qGIvtw==>  clients have spent $100 million on the platform so far. Native Win

 

BuzzFeed aims to bank $120 million in revenue next year, according to Ad Age, and if the numbers are correct, that would be double their revenue from this year. A spokeswoman declined to comment but told Ad Age the company is profitable. BuzzFeed has raised $46 million to date, and relies on revenue solely from native ads. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001sGUmN75PH-Ri7nFsXtKx5DhLIiPyLJ-qny86Gzp8UCSrp4TOeqQY2oPwh2-Z3buF-aFuROcRlY9ocue7oUgp6eGMoZ2CaJHDJdf0zYmFwAsi0doYx5g2b-s1AYPIias4_wjQUzP9GfuQuxOh6p4yAi4ggGmAzco18DvK7B-bNba0fItmIqEkbk-nbk1XwVsNTKGFxCpjukE=> .

 

India Ad Market

 

India has the third largest "Internet population," according to comScore, which has new analysis of the growing market. The auto and finance ad categories are seeing dramatic growth, with retail and consumer goods also surging. As with the United States, Amazon, Google and Microsoft are among the top advertisers in the country. OLX has the top spot. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001sGUmN75PH-T_Y7uMIKmf1mHM2AU80QHDbalrLVBu-s3i8kAGAcIYIl5XPUIgyjycow2tO1-R7ZN0D2BhISFuCo88gPL0x-9SIAFNUlZRJ_fpV3PZrhDk_9NdAK5oeRlEsEKzIpFRvCFfZFKbPLbtUUq6dsO-PI5hPF9wmXbrwOhjuMT9OtFgPeYukgwsK8-CK9SZLqIi8Y-kntFJb9OGQg==> .

IAB Talks Native

 

The IAB is stepping into the native ads standardization process, releasing a playbook for publishers, agencies and marketers <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NDBtS1Z_76xGCr1_8RITmrc-AqA-ygBjoY_dFp1j-ysbWAoz9nOMJeFAXAHwzOvBYogahaqqIvy4XOfSXa8XVgLw3qVzhq2LLe39Bqq_Gz_05X-UdWdnr8jRLrugFcUV> . According to the IAB, the six formats considered native advertising are: in-feed units, paid search units, recommendation widgets, promoted listings, IAB standard ads with "native" element units and custom. There will be a workshop in March to further address the native ad landscape. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NDBtS1Z_76wavGS1FA_4QaX6apoBMHEnC70mC-vaY0fYoOglJ3cYosZkz-ZZr1sJOPHNo4G0_V2WFuKWspvPg0wb3srb_hy2mKop1RVNEytKVLsPa2WBITI4rYkXsiY4j70Yimz4PcGFlSh7RLjXkZfvc3kNcsRIXYa0Y7aTzsXTgKIj5KX8Y-tBOOTOxwD2V9_eR67XJuz_Qi3uuE-dkg80KqGPtLHqRvub0P-Dm44=> .

 

Twitter Retargeting

 

TechCrunch's John Constine says his sources tell him Twitter retargeting is on its way. He adds, "The secret sauce of Twitter's retargeting is the use of your account as a cross-device identity layer, allowing it to target ads on mobile based on where you've been on the web." Read more on how it may work. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NDBtS1Z_76zE04bPAI3YRfDhrPsRI0uF2mpRdQvzqKWQcznYmezRmaNYcVC8fsa91scNtugzbV4OTv44JC7UbJvsjbH3xdwE9imEyLPBcJqKVG4VB8TUhpX1iJpp_5LCsCfYWWshPdKiamqN8_FR-CLfWGVg4IU_DKA_vitymyw=>  Triggit CEO Zach Coelius tells Constine, "Twitter is in a unique position because people log in on both the web and phone." 

 

Data-Driven Team-Up

 

Big data giant Acxiom and media agency Starcom MediaVest Group (SMG) have swung a long-term deal in which SMG will be the first agency to use Acxiom's new Audience Operating System <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NDBtS1Z_76xmy5oK2IH083A9qVFbrNyIRRqeGItUP5XmUmpt5CvjuFOeehx38bwIRHuaOmezrq6yfqAvop4e-CQBmhC9EqEkreXycDq8-X5-YTvnsvNT-mJIsdKbMW6zZBJcHVzUxOKWLaFjS4Z9fzva_JKwkCRkxPjfL_4NJ2jb5zd7WwJr_RVNu4HkF9cNYBNyHiO7PCWOtSqsDICr0-Rigmr3lu7OEsvjCwwDjho=>  (AOS). In the DMP competitive set, Acxiom positions its AOS differentiation as the collection and aggregation of both online and offline data. With the Acxiom and SMG deal, the two companies hope to work together to develop new data-sharing applications that will work with AOS. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NDBtS1Z_76woif2V4hEQKA3NtdR_IVsd89b6mweo8uivftiKAChT0HnGWNUbidUYiXf1H7AIuJt4612_2DEFkzPovp9gY-xERPqgoBVGYfC5bT7f9FGUmzjNIH2eHNzKixAQzIH0Z16goCexQl8kre_g1H9mnh-nq3WC-WFQw_dyvoiKkDsj3X0mfigBcMRReJmxUpXD6vgbXJB8R2fV_SteybiJM6mM-Z1aAywNZfk=> .

 

Mail Exchange

 

Germany-based Internet portal company United Internet Media is collaborating with AppNexus to create an exchange, the company announced. Germany has a rapidly growing real-time advertising marketing, and the IDC predicts it will account for one in five euros spent on display ads by 2015. The United Internet portals include GMX, WEB.DE, mail.com (all mail service) and 1&1. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NDBtS1Z_76xOTZd6PyQjNlv9hCCyqE9j9bPwXM193cXsu4wpOnFOvIjmxwhZM8x-0VXDL_KetNvj7zx6s2_Qu0SaaWXrpb5Hv82QOLBoNv6eD7TEb_4rx91sQ4MGtg51EokTJ78dbZb4rAMrfZHeULDDTTUNtbDtggY1CHElup-PBuhS0X0gANjZ_rciu3Yj0hhIce0Mbx86CoE92Ej9kfUDSkZVw47e> .

 

Bad Bots

 

Spider.io has been working to uncover the truth about the unscrupulous practice of buying and selling fraudulent traffic. Its latest effort is an in-depth look at how bots infect a computer, falsely interact with Web pages and, ultimately, interact with ads. Spider.io calls out what it sees at the offenders taking part in traffic fraud. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NDBtS1Z_76wifElBzyqhKB6uMHpmAty9IuXFpJUjmC09lQ42_a9_hl6XHFb4lmJKPq5HCg27xsw7OpdugSM5IqU_xCEH8utRbMsAZU8DIfUEEwn7hNZYoHNFgnqHweaa6J_Zala4C5u2_1OSyaHm_MnXQNeZ6xZ4zt_YxHLV2p5X4du7kXeFHpUew8-0-npgI0P6cWzqZrM9RSPrn97zQg==> .

Data Hype

 

After taking a closer look at data-driven marketing, Upstream Group empresario Doug Weaver concludes...he's not so impressed. There are still some lingering issues that make the ecosystem more like a karaoke bar than a concert (his analogy). Some of the major hurdles are an overreliance on retargeting, lack of quality in third-party data, fraud and cross-platform issues. Read the post <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NDBtS1Z_76zGdNwk8_6l37F3tu0s1T7pBIw5eDbjvQA4Yd7QToLpfm_y-M4eRW2RR9UKgOWjTeWYKLO4wvMU54qH04p8KzOksPZhMFPlzoDQjaGW2NCABrbLYU32kmOwxecmTsZAXLHvsklwfqXkSg==> .

 

Network Strategy

 

A new GigaOM research report by Lydia Loizides focuses on LinkedIn's business strategy post-IPO, especially since it didn't meet expectations in Q3 2013. The report looks at LinkedIn's focus on its product, its disregard for talent solutions and its acquisition strategy. Read the report <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NDBtS1Z_76wWGdKSjeWsTheNhAeJbYi4Bju2agmuxEsDijTqr1JpHcUyJxf8wv-t7Dk_OliuT7Rb7N4URF-7yAtX5ZmsN5VufgVnhyYDIfYG3NUec5PIjuXF6b3bN0ife3pjKUpT2hBEPsSzVs_wnUQ2x1XrXu_wFn85umO3Eog_YBmTTG38ZCqb9A4DnowELguBrvaJeP8=>  (subscription).

 

Shopping Habits

 

According to research done by Millward Brown Digital and published in Adweek, mobile shoppers visit more retailer sites than those on a PC and are more likely to shop around. Mobile shoppers are also most active on the weekends and at night, but tablet users prefer that platform over mobile at home. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NDBtS1Z_76yBSD1X61JMQjf_IqeqhbQnLmrtHD3X2ccMCVtydKzayU7CcQN71Pmo2KjZ98gk7hEIDo5qZRs2cKvS_hMpE6FA_JExdradSX-uaEtlLXbqnS3UpPyQ-sCJKQWNP9gKWrHxZI_ZlJVuvfaFJnp1m3YJ98Al0n_EKS_DAV3CuGLS0BWIcDuN6KckflEhvhIHWTD1qxrLaqxsCMpGisSVYPGs> .

LiveRail On Growth Rate

 

LiveRail hopes to differentiate itself from video ad networks that have already gone public by its growth rate, according to TechCrunch's Anthony Ha. LiveRail tells Ha it's growing at a 200% run rate this year. "For LiveRail, being on pace for $100 million in revenues puts it almost on par with those who have gone before it. YuMe is expecting full-year revenue to be in a range of $154.5 million and $157.5 million, while Tremor's full-year guidance is for between $125 million and $126 million." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ms-_kXibZPti5tP81Gj6Tot_OThpB84Z7kd5naMxJ7TOV6zAPIQfaJWUjQV3WFa8V0qmZHV4-skJAqZODPbic-VruRytkqXzYKmpdQbi0h0ghyguQ9YpaLL56nl6T9X8y-JONnhCDYxZRzmft-9k6U5iczy7HNqV_1AXVT5VozDPAYgKClbS6A==> . An IPO in the second half of 2014 is possible, says LiveRail. And read the momentum release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ms-_kXibZPtlZWv3Knn45HieUvTBZlPFcrLxKtY5WRyD5RnvgIDfNAgh8shrf7flo50mFxTkEFVdLXwin0mjBOaslX2Geos8dS9DPk172DI36HqQuEnyn_g8Tf1WojubvNnr5SL2BM9o3AhazR4qPgd2HQgoDHYnJykf4nM7IzmVgShyAXHm5BsgU_rnoO6Ot5Mw2EHZfHdSB8KIszGd1ldKtYEOlDAG9jvBIons_grZxQTuQLBmMcffBlAdKwMwv0nK8yz3U8w=> .

 

Pay Up

 

A study conducted by the ANA found that 43% of marketers have extended payment terms, and 57% of those who extended payments reported a strained vendor relationship. The finance department and/or procurement and purchasing were responsible for the majority of payment term changes. "While the ANA does not recommend any specific term or practice, we do advocate better collaboration that advances the quality of the marketer/supplier relationship and the products and services delivered," says Bob Liodice, president and CEO of ANA. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ms-_kXibZPv8XeLvYelqK87ayLKZdOqcLZV8EMohXBNGpKoC7Lco84oIuNKIeNSZKtObgew_sy4dpMcQt6kpekFASGO-Hp1vHkaK1RV9qaAACZ9punJ9XPdqI1NARFpDS4HV-STiOOKP2AViMK2MqQ==> .

 

Believing In Programmatic

 

In a blog post, entrepreneur and new Mozilla exec <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ms-_kXibZPudXQmOSxWMPa1PYxmIOYdsGq1UbAwtdlFTGb5uWuJuwcDwZauC6ucG98V69-1zrJk23Gv2tKCHrBMUzAahvYqNYlAxTGjxc9_68qOi4TH3oSH1dNYy8ce3LNUgMHt8-bQ2gFay7L0WZjlgehFApVDO7B41agXmWjBHaLS4c2UlRVF_UknDO_2VkU4gKOkvxCeMyyWzi9W8ibKxxvLPLFKmENsjF3aHzKU=>  Darren Herman outlines why he's increasingly bullish about programmatic media. With more focus on business and vision over features, open innovation and accountability, programmatic is becoming a natural part of the advertising process. Herman writes, "Lastly, I'm bullish on programmatic media because we're going outside of media for the programmatic conversation. ... In some of the investment circles that I'm in, we're discussing the businesses outside of advertising that are being transformed programmatically. This, at least to me, is very exciting." Read the post <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ms-_kXibZPvKx9EIW-wzA-Ilny3aGVgEI65sW57DYwiFB4qWvU3BKNQhy_TZsf5KqYU9nS60BQGi3rLXnjTIJRMdC-bhWtNGWUWiUqF0VZ8wFO2hXzKmNuuh4Xohyo38z6tYYKmSUV3JJIZp0gZ7oh929Q2o2_G6XFQzM1wa8jyQJSpaiJ-zSDoYwjv8Cm6VA0LnCXRAIII=> .

 

Cross-Device Patent

 

Mobile ad company Adelphic has won a patent for "user identification on network-connected devices," according to a press release. The list of devices includes smartphones, tablets and PCs. "Identifying users across devices and media is the foundation of data-driven audience engagement." says Changfeng Wang, CTO and co-founder of Adelphic, in the release. "The advertising industry needs to go beyond cookies toward a mechanism that works well with existing technology and user privacy guidelines." Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ms-_kXibZPs_adLSwwONqOlUF6JkoTe96VD2VnDPrVZI4ZSR16crsOc1bnT4Lz6h0_wYJYYE8Ue1cn6iSFRkLiiQY_D5ZJRGwQ9zyi5w8iSLD6CbcdChGFlwWweknDejZw8OPmcmtNyzL5l_IF7DTe7UjNejPZpwtgIz2uSGuWU=> .

 

Don't Cut Out The Middleman

 

Jayne Pimentel, director of demand sales at Nexage, lends her thoughts on self-serve platforms, and why they may not be necessary, echoing Joanna O'Connell's thoughts <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ms-_kXibZPvSFJjuW0cGwU2UC4WfC6Hc_9avqcOBU8oMHZzikMDVX2fbEMDXX-z7ZFEcxtnsDffjr8dbRKigraJDrTyyoZUQ7gywNJNDCALJfCtdclxrhY7uJyPwWf-GVeg_aXs8dUx_EyIXnu3Jcuzm8sLh5Ux9kFOwBdA2MHbLA5NCQoiOuC5z78beuiLNqYzRyEddWa414J_bJJ1ZTRORZvtw18tbwY80lL8NhwS2d0rxyaSOTQ==> . Pimentel's arguments center on the cost, work flow and specialist aspects of a self-service platform, and comes out in favor of using middlemen, such as agencies, over taking it in-house. She writes, "If self-serve is your ticket to cutting costs then think about the executional layer, billing and technical aspects before you ditch your agency. If you're providing the self-serve services -- create a consulting layer. Not just a troubleshooting layer." Read the post <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ms-_kXibZPtDOMjY1XTpee2-gIVJr2Rw9FPhly5o0RUs36u2OPI_0-JfCvAS3Hl4KAye5petLnBopCTxg1FvNZd49xYWWkKF6tQefA-QVwtiBclHQlx25kyC5SFt7akcvDZpJ6I0CV77rf_WKWFaGx497WhieSO14JvgNjjts99zTk1NF_MovBdrYB6Bk7valuVDq66qrIakaoglB_npEg==> .

Networks Alive And Well

 

Ad networks aren't dead. In fact, they're doing just fine, according to Jeff Hirsch, CMO of CPX Interactive. In a column for MediaPost, Hirsch points to the wave of IPOs this year that featured companies operating like ad networks (Tremor, YuMe, Rocket Fuel and Criteo) as evidence for his position. He writes, "It's time to stop pronouncing the death of the ad network and realize that not only are they here to stay -- these companies provide a valuable service to both advertisers and publishers." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ms-_kXibZPvy8CLGHjKrNFERVaFXRIwkiaYyWPNnARpSCIJXFfKkwhTezNnODf4RGrFVOupU6HrLXlgHogHI9zRx9nV6cMWRLWOFhAf5Bj_D_QGsWbS4TATGUab2g1nqNtsGtR0lAgjmR993zAfTy6nF4zoMjNwIV6ePy2C-6K2kCoy64Sko2NbSpcO2ObZnskvkCBt_Gn705LCuoXcBSyebBMUzngn-KB_NSt_zFIM=> .
